    Posted on: 2023-04-07; at: 16:23

    @vishal_singh @DataEngPodcast However, as Vishal rightly points out, not every interaction with data should be treated as a product. It's important to understand when you need to add contextual attributes and when you don't.

    Posted on: 2023-04-07; at: 16:23

    @vishal_singh @DataEngPodcast To implement data as a product approach is to ask what problems you want to solve, who will use the data and why, and what iterations are needed. This process mirrors a product cycle: capture the idea, create the solution, get feedback, and ideate again.

    Posted on: 2023-04-07; at: 16:23

    ➡️ The Outbox pattern addresses the transactional guarantee of events and ensures consistency while modifying the transactional database.

    Posted on: 2023-04-12; at: 14:06

    ➡️ There are three types of architectural patterns in data creation: Event Sourcing, Change Data Capture, and Outbox pattern. Each pattern has its limitations and drawbacks, and companies must choose the one that best suits their needs.

    Posted on: 2023-04-12; at: 14:06
